<Rating>1< /Rating><review>Interesting...  I posted a review on 2/3/17 on Yelp and they took it down and blocked me from posting reviews on their site.  Apparently the corporate guy got pissed I called him out.  No wonder their reviews have been so good lately, they just block and take down the bad ones on Yelp.

2/3/17
I used to frequent this store on a regular basis and hadn't been in for a while.  I was in just before Christmas again.  The appearance of the store looks much better, cleaner, more modern, etc.  However, it seems to have a major identity crisis.  They now seem to have small selections of various types of products but really not much selection of each.  They now carry lingerie and mens underwear, but that has taken away from the space they used to have more toy and hard core selections.  But, that being said, its now a place that I thought my new girlfriend would be comfortable going to.  So, I took her last evening.  We browsed around hoping she'd find something she'd like, which would mean I could maybe get something I'd like.  She wasn't impressed either.  I was hoping she'd find some lingerie and then I could maybe introduce her to a harder core product.  Wasn't the case.  On both visits the sales staff were not nearly as helpful of knowledgable about the products as they were years ago.  When I was there several weeks ago there was a guy in the store yelling at and down right rude to several employees.  I happened to ask who he was when purchasing some lube and was told he's from corporate.  Sadly, not the friendly, knowledgable store with great selection it used to be.< /review><pictures>None</pictures>< Response>

< review>
just thinking about Dave's hot chicken makes me want Dave's hot chicken.

So so good.  The chicken is always so juicy and tender, which is rare for white meat.

One thing to note is that the heat levels aren't evenly spaced, meaning mild to medium isn't that big of a difference but medium to hot is a huge difference in terms of spiciness.

Be prepared to wait half an hour plus to eat, but one can almost always find seating, esp if you're a small party.

Portions are huge, especially for fries so consider sharing.

Parking can sometimes be difficult so be prepared to wait a little.< /review>

<Text>The bulgogi was unseasoned and the prices were outrageous, at least to my sensibilities. By having such large and expensive portion sizes, it is impossible to have the mix and match kbbq experience I have known and loved for so long. I really feel like I only got $40 of food, 50 at most, and another 10 of service, but it came out to more than double that, plus tip. I'm not even comparing it to cheap podunk hometown rates, for the amount of money I paid, KBBQ shops in Las Vegas can get you three times as much food, better quality overall, and you can try different things. I don't want to pay 30 dollars for a single pound of just one preparation of meat, I'd much rather pay 10 bucks each for 3 kinds. The desert cannot be split by fewer than 3 people, so I feel like at least I get good value from that, but the meat is where it counts, and I could've spent that money better. < text>
Been here a few times after golfing at Mather.  The food is good.  I've sampled a few of their pizza's and found them all satisfying.  The flavor is above average imho.  The crust is not real thin but I suspect you could get it that way if you asked.  Prices are fair and staff is very friendly and helpful.  Overall, i get the impression they care a lot about their pizza and how much you enjoy it.

Plenty of seating both inside and out.  Inside is very spacious and can get a little on the cool side. Outside is relaxing in good weather. In place of video games, you can take a board game to your table.  Honestly,  I enjoy that since it encourages more interaction.  I haven't tried enough things on their menu but intend to do so in the future.

If you're done playing 18 holes at Mather and need a place for a good pizza and a brew, this is the place to go.<//text>

<Text>This is specifically for the Soquel Avenue location. This is one of the best taquerias in town and I'm always amazed that it doesn't make the "best of" lists published. The carna asada has SO much flavor. The tacos are delicious and packed full of meat. I'd highly recommend the carne asada tacos, any variety of the super burritos (but especially the shrimp), the cheese enchiladas, and the tostado. Prices are fairly reasonable, but they've gone up lately. Parking is easy to find and the restaurant itself is huge with plenty of tables. They have a salsa bar with amazing pico de gayo and serve fresh chips with every order. There's a selection of Mexican beverages and desserts. The interior is a little worn, and some menu items are pricier than others. Really love this place.<//Text><date>1525583869488< /date>< Resp>

<review>Reading these reviews I have come to the following conclusions:
1. This place has excellent tacos. Order them.
2. Get the Al Pastor as your meat choice.
3. Don't order veggie here. (Or at any taqueria really. I mean c'mon.)
4. If you're acting privileged you will be treated accordingly. Smile and be respectful.
5. Be prepared to spend a little more than you'd like, but the Al Pastor tacos will make you glad you did.
6. If all else fails order the soup. The soup is the best thing on the menu.
7. Whatever you order get it to go, make sure to check it over before you leave, like any thinking person would.
Enjoy!</review></record>
